API - To get Access/Bearer token.
URL - http://localhost:3003/auth/getToken
METHOD - POST
BODY - { clientKey: "a35c1234ebc332ce815c4cd988c4bec3X0UIBxueE2vvMLAgzjcF5w==" }
RESPONSE - {
    "message": "success",
    "status": 1,
    "data": {
        "updateAvailable": false,
        "releaseNote": "",
        "message": "Token assigned",
        "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpZCI6eyJyZWdpc3Rlcl9pZCI6NzgwLCJtYWNfYWRkcmVzcyI6IjMwOjljOjIzOmUwOjc5OjdlIiwib3NfdHlwZSI6IlVidW50dSBMaW51eCIsImNsaWVudF9rZXkiOiJhMzVjMTIzNGViYzMzMmNlODE1YzRjZDk4OGM0YmVjM1gwVUlCeHVlRTJ2dk1MQWd6amNGNXc9PSIsInBsYW5fc3RhcnRfZGF0ZSI6IjIwMjItMTEtMjMgMDQ6NDY6MzkiLCJwbGFuX2V4cGlyZSI6IjIwMjEtMTItMzEgMTE6NTk6NTkiLCJzdWJzY3JpcHRpb25fcGxhbiI6Miwic3VwcG9ydF9wbGFuIjozLCJtZXNzYWdlIjoiU3VjY2Vzc2Z1bGwiLCJzdGF0dXMiOjEsImh0dHBTdGF0dXNDb2RlIjoyMDAsIm9zVHlwZSI6IlVidW50dSBMaW51eCJ9LCJpYXQiOjE2NzA1MDAxMjcsImV4cCI6MTY3MDU4NjUyN30.NvLbCh_6cDFlGnpdLqb1V23tLI78EA7LHCopc6GLSzs"

############################################################################################################################

(On click on connection icon in create cluster screen)
Note: For Master Node, type:1, For Worker Node, type:2
API - To create a VM.

URL - http://localhost:3003/vm
METHOD - POST
BODY - {
    description: "master1",
    ip: "18.182.230.58",
    password: "Admin#$2022@Fabdep",
    type: 1,
    username: "ubuntu",
}
RESPONSE - {
   "message":"success",
   "status":1,
   "data":{
      "type":1,
      "status":1,
      "_id":"6399a1b917c72bb6d0a0afa0",
      "ip":"18.182.230.58",
      "__v":0,
      "created_at":"2022-12-14T10:13:13.161Z",
      "description":"master1",
      "password":"Fabdep@Dev#$321",
      "updated_at":"2022-12-14T10:13:13.161Z",
      "username":"ubuntu"
   }
}

############################################################################################################################

API - To create a cluster.
URL - http://localhost:3003/cluster
METHOD - POST
BODY - {
   "description":"cluster1",
   "master_node":"6399a1b917c72bb6d0a0afa0",
   "name":"cluster1"
}
RESPONSE - {
    "message": "Cluster has been created!",
    "data": {
        "worker_node": [],
        "status": 1,
        "_id": "63a16146927d3da67973b981",
        "name": "cluster1",
        "master_node": "63a1607817c72bb6d0a434c1",
        "description": "cluster1",
        "created_at": "2022-12-20T07:16:22.231Z",
        "updated_at": "2022-12-20T07:16:22.231Z",
        "__v": 0
    }
}

API - To setup worker.
URL - http://localhost:3003/cluster/worker
METHOD - POST
BODY - {
    "cluster_id": "63a16146927d3da67973b981",
    "worker_vm_id": "63a160b317c72bb6d0a434e1"
}
RESPONSE - {
    "message": "Worker node has been added to the cluster!",

API - To Add Organization (Any - Orderer or Peer) (type: 1 for Orderer Org & type: 0 for Peer Org)

API - To save Channel Info
URL - http://localhost:3003/channel/saveChannelInfo
METHOD - POST
BODY - {
    "name": "mychannel",
    "operators": ["63a2a059139d99d92c8906b7", "63a2ac7d139d99d92c8906ba"],
    "ordererserviceId": "63a2afab139d99d92c8906bd"
}

      "type":0,
